	OutputLine(NULL, "…………ない。",
		   NULL, " tinha desaparecido.", Line_ContinueAfterTyping);

	SetValidityOfInput( FALSE );

	SetValidityOfInput( TRUE );

		   NULL, " ...Desaparecido.", Line_ContinueAfterTyping);

	SetValidityOfInput( FALSE );
	Wait( 1000 );

	OutputLine(NULL, "ない。",
		   NULL, " Desaparecido.", Line_Normal);

	PlayBGM( 1, "msys16", 56, 0 );
//　じゃあ......俺は、............一体、何を...＠

	OutputLine(NULL, "　じゃあ……俺は、…………一体、何を…。",
		   NULL, "Então... o que diabos...... eu estava...", GetGlobalFlag(GLinemodeSp));

	if (GetGlobalFlag(GADVMode)) { OutputLineAll("", NULL, Line_ContinueAfterTyping); }

//　そんなはずはない＠...絶対にあれは現実だった＠幻であるわけがない＠
	if (GetGlobalFlag(GADVMode)) { OutputLineAll("", NULL, Line_ContinueAfterTyping); }

		   NULL, "Não podia ser isso.", Line_WaitForInput);

		   NULL, "Eu o matei.", Line_WaitForInput);

	if (GetGlobalFlag(GADVMode)) { OutputLineAll("", NULL, Line_ContinueAfterTyping); }
